<pictures>None<//pictures>< review>
For three days during the month of September there is what is known as a "Stand Down". During this event Veterans from every branch of the United States Armed Forces come together for a 3 day retreat. Food, clothing, fun, music and access to plenty of resources provided by plenty of agencies geared towards veterans  support.
It's a great experience and show of community based support for veteran's who have served in the Armed Forces Of America.< /review>

Clam appetizer and Risotto with chef's choice of fish. The appetizer was good. Lots of clams, both with the shell and without. A pink sauce with tomato chunks. Next time I'll try something different.
The risotto had 4 perfectly grilled shrimp, chunks of fish, veggies, mushrooms, and more. However, I couldn't really taste a risotto, more like a rice dish. Good but not what I was expecting.

Service was great. I'll try it again.<//review>

Truly authentic Italian food. Cannot say enough about the consistency and deliciousness of this restaurant. If you are used to American, garbage Italian, go to Olive Garden or Bocco de Beppo. But if you love real Italian food, VinoSanto will not disappoint. From starters to dessert, we walked out feeling blissful as we do on holidays at our family gatherings. <user_name>Giovanni Faonte< /user_name><time>1552803104327</time>< rate>

< text>
One of the worse food experiences in my life. Our order was: calamari, polenta, veal saltimbocca and linguine with clams. The calamari were obviously frozen given their tender consistency and lack of taste. Polenta was ok, but adding feta on top is really not Italian. Veal saltimbocca tasted of condensed broth, trick cheap restaurants use to mask the freshness and taste of ingredients and preparation. The pasta with clams was the worse and potentially the most dangerous for your well being: it tasted also like condensed broth and had a lot of extra clams off their shell that were obviously added after from maybe not fresh seafood preserves. The clams were off their natural shape and potentially the condensed broth taste covered the not freshness of the seafood which could cause serious illnesses. i am myself from Italy and they cannot easily trick me on food. Perhaps more vulnerable/less experienced customers will be caught into the trap. If you are not willing to respect the Italian standards of food quality and tradition do not be on the market and charge like  an authentic italian restaurant. You are screwing the Italian food credibility by doing that. For the records, we got charged 100$ which in many other real italian places would provide you a real italian experience.<//text>

Cafe Sparrow has an unassuming store front, but the atmosphere inside is elegant and welcoming.  It has a long record of dedication to quality dishes and fresh food.  The menu changes daily and they always offer a variety that includes something for everyone. They are renowned for their pork chops, but the fish and beef prep is on par. Sparrow also offers an interesting variety of wines. The French influence is present in every aspect. This is my go to for special occasions and one of the best restaurants in the bay area.</Review>

<name>Reed Welch< /name>< Text>
A special occasion made better

My wife and I returned to Cafe Sparrow in celebration of our wedding anniversary. It turned out to be a candlelight dinner via mother nature. The electrical power went out while we were enjoying out starters. The staff didn‚Äôt miss a beat, as extra candles were brought to the tables. The full house of patrons were at ease and all appeared to enjoy the experience.

This is probably our 6th visit to Cafe Sparrow in the past 4 years, and we have not been disappointed. I had the Chicken livers, which were prepared with apples, bacon, and garlic, without any of the condiments being overwhelming, and mixing nicely with the chicken liver. My wife had the special risotto with beef dish. We paired these with a Zinfandel from their wine list, and sat back and enjoyed a wonderful evening.
Even under the handicap of no power, the kitchen was able to provide their wonderful desserts.

This will be an evening that we will remember for quite some time.....<//Text>

Here is the story, almost unbelievable, sad but true:

50 minutes into the meal, became concerned about the entrees arrival. Expressed my concern to waitress, and I was told " oh, you should have told me you needed to leave so soon" (Evidently, I incorrectly thought that 1 hr and 15 minutes was enough time for a meal with a very early reservation and only 3 other tables seated!)

My immediate thought was "she forgot to put in our ticket, or the kitchen is backed up"

1 hr and 5 minutes after prompt arrival, still no entree, so, we had to leave because I was taking my 10 year daughter to a movie on our special night out. No way to enjoy entr√©e at this late juncture.

Interestingly, and surprising to me, I was told by wait person later "we usually allow 1 hr 45 minutes per couple." If this was Le Cirque, Le Bernardin, or the French Laundry, I guess that would be the norm, but this is a casual venue in sleepy Aptos. Really!
